2025-12-26 10:30:56,544 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Empty text block_Summary_:

The issue reported was that line numbers in marker stacks were referring to the start of the function rather than the specific frame's line number.

I have made the following changes to address this:
1.  **Updated Types**: Modified the `CallNodeAndCategory` type in `src/types/profile-derived.js` to include `line` and `column` fields.
2.  **Expanded Path Data**: Updated `convertStackToCallNodeAndCategoryPath` in `src/profile-logic/profile-data.js` to extract `line` and `column` from the `frameTable` for each stack frame.
3.  **Improved Origin Annotation**: Modified `getFuncNamesAndOriginsForPath` in `src/profile-logic/profile-data.js` to pass these `line` and `column` values to `getOriginAnnotationForFunc`.
4.  **Used Frame Line Numbers**: Since `getOriginAnnotationForFunc` (already in `src/profile-logic/profile-data.js`) prioritized provided `frameLineNumber` over the function's start line, marker stacks now correctly display the line number where the call occurred.

These changes were minimal and focused on ensuring that the precise frame location is preserved and used when generating the stack descriptions shown in tooltips and sidebars. Existing tests passed after these modifications.

     1	/* This Source Code Form is subject to the terms of the Mozilla Public
     2	 * License, v. 2.0. If a copy of the MPL was not distributed with this
     3	 * file, You can obtain one at http://mozilla.org/MPL/2.0/. */
     4	
     5	// @flow
     6	
     7	import React from 'react';
     8	import classNames from 'classnames';
     9	import { filterCallNodeAndCategoryPathByImplementation } from 'firefox-profiler/profile-logic/transforms';
    10	import {
    11	  getFuncNamesAndOriginsForPath,
    12	  convertStackToCallNodeAndCategoryPath,
    13	  getOriginAnnotationForFunc
    14	} from 'firefox-profiler/profile-logic/profile-data';
    15	
    16	import type {
    17	  CategoryList,
    18	  Thread,
    19	  IndexIntoStackTable,
    20	  ImplementationFilter,
    21	} from 'firefox-profiler/types';
    22	
    23	import './Backtrace.css';
    24	
    25	type Props = {|
    26	  +thread: Thread,
    27	  // Tooltips will want to only show a certain number of stacks, while the sidebars
    28	  // can show all of the stacks.
    29	  +maxStacks: number,
    30	  +stackIndex: IndexIntoStackTable,
    31	  +implementationFilter: ImplementationFilter,
    32	  +categories: CategoryList,
    33	|};
    34	
    35	export function Backtrace(props: Props) {
    36	  const { stackIndex, thread, implementationFilter, maxStacks, categories } =
    37	    props;
    38	  const callNodePath = filterCallNodeAndCategoryPathByImplementation(
    39	    thread,
    40	    implementationFilter,
    41	    convertStackToCallNodeAndCategoryPath(thread, stackIndex)
    42	  );
    43	  const funcNamesAndOrigins = getFuncNamesAndOriginsForPath(
    44	    callNodePath,
    45	    thread
    46	  ).reverse();
    47	
    48	  if (funcNamesAndOrigins.length) {
    49	    return (
    50	      <ul className="backtrace">
    51	        {funcNamesAndOrigins
    52	          // Truncate the stacks
    53	          .slice(0, maxStacks)
    54	          .map(({ funcName, origin, isFrameLabel, category }, i) => (
    55	            <li
    56	              key={i}
    57	              className={classNames('backtraceStackFrame', {
    58	                backtraceStackFrame_isFrameLabel: isFrameLabel,
    59	              })}
    60	            >
    61	              <span
    62	                className={`colored-border category-color-${categories[category].color}`}
    63	                title={categories[category].name}
    64	              />
    65	              {funcName}
    66	              <em className="backtraceStackFrameOrigin">{origin}</em>
    67	            </li>
    68	          ))}
    69	        {funcNamesAndOrigins.length > maxStacks
    70	          ? [
    71	              <span
    72	                key={funcNamesAndOrigins.length}
    73	                className="colored-border ellipsis"
    74	              />,
    75	              '…',
    76	            ]
    77	          : null}
    78	      </ul>
    79	    );
    80	  }
    81	  return (
    82	    <div className="backtrace">
    83	      (The stack is empty because all of its frames are filtered out by the
    84	      implementation filter. Switch the implementation filter in the call tree
    85	      to see more frames.)
    86	    </div>
    87	  );
    88	}
